To me it smells like BDC + ginger ale. This is a summer / spring banger and I will continue to wear this in fall / winter if I'm expected to be in door a lot (party, wedding, etc).<br />
<br />
Projection and longevity is solid, it keeps you in a nice scent bubble for as long as 8h-10h, but I'm surprised no one is talking about how much the atomizer dispenses. 1 spray from bottle is like 3 equal sprays from the samples so please take that into consideration if you're using samples or decants. I think a lot of the mix reviews we have been seeing with LV fragrances are caused by the inconsistency between samples, decants, and og bottle atomizer (longevity / projection).<br />
<br />
Overall, this is a very safe non offensive "BLEU" fragrance that has it's own twist. I will continue to refill this bottle if it runs out. I can see someone wearing this as their signature scent all year round.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="2263825"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=2263825#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2261850" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; 1) This sparkles with body heat, previously I used this here in Bogot√° (constantly 10 centigrades, Autumn like weather). In this conditions the fragrance results in a sour dry citrus; however, using this in the gym, the heat helped radiating the watery grapefruit, really refreshing and invigorating.<br />

2) To me, Cavellier mixed 2 of his fragrances to get this: Bvlgari Aqva Amara and Bvlgari tygar. It has the refreshing sour watery aspects of Amara, without that seaweed like note; mixed with the great grapefruit and ambroxan of Tygar.<br />

<br />
 Longevity is great, it lasts 10h on me, projecting strongly during the initial 4-5 hours.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2134270" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Augustus857"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1794732"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1794732.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Augustus857" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Orientica-Premium/Xclusif-Oud-Bleu-78036.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78036.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Xclusif Oud Bleu"title="Xclusif Oud Bleu"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2134270ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2134270" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1794732">Augustus857</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-23">04/23/24 18:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THIS IS A QUICK COMPARISON BETWEEN<br />
<br />
Masion Alhambra Immortal <br />
And<br />
Flavia L'Impression <br />
And<br />
Alexandria Fragrances L'immensity <br />
And <br />
The original Louis Vuitton L'immensit√© (decant)<br />
<br />
They are all very close but not accurate <br />
<br />
L'Impression is the closest in the opening, but in the dry down is softer and becomes a skin scent but still very close. If you want the most accurate clone down to how soft the original becomes in the dry down, get the Flavia L'Impression clone, just spray a bit more. 90% close in opening, 85% close in dry down.<br />
<br />
Immortal is VERY ginger forward in the opening, but becomes closer in the dry down with a ginger focus but has better overall performance than Impression and even L'immensit√©. If you really love ginger then get Masion Alhambra Immortal clone. 80% close in opening, 85% close in dry down.<br />
<br />
L'immensity is in the middle to overall closeness it's just slightly more grapefruit forward in the opening and becomes closer in the dry down with a grapefruit focus, but since it's an extrate it has the best longevity, sillage and projection than all of them. If you want slightly more grapefruit and beast mode performance Alexandria Fragrance L'immensity clone. 85% close in opening, 90% close in the dry down.<br />
<br />
L'immensit√© is an awesome fragrance, very balanced, with average longevity, sillage and projection, it's very well done, but the $280 to $320 price tag is pretty steep. If Brand name is important and you got the money then get the Louis Vuitton. Performance is average to below average for it's hefty price tag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="2134270"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=2134270#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2125590" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It develops into a masculine &amp; fruity concoction which at times makes me reminisce of Millesime Imperial by Creed, although not smelling alike, just in terms of vibe. This is a phenomenal frag with pretty decent performance to boot!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="2108531"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=2108531#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104447" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Out of them all L'immensit√© caught my eye the most. Is it the most unique fragrance out of them all? Short answer, no. In the start i get hit by this fresh grapefruit and then a bit later in the dry down i get the ginger. As mentioned before me, L'immensit√© has this barbershop vibe to it. It smells like you walk in to this barbershop in the 90s on a summer day while still keeping that masculine everyday scent vibe. I actually really enjoy this scent even though it's "simplicity" and i am contemplating picking up a bottle of this but i have to try it out a couple more times.<br />
<br />
Edit: flash forward to present day where i've just picked up a bottle of this heavenly juice. I am absolutely in love with this scent. It's to the point where i don't even bother spraying it on my wrist anymore, just because of the fact that i can't stop smelling my wrist which leads to me going nose blind after 20 minutes of applying it. Hands down my favorite from Louis Vuitton with more than decent longevity and projection.<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="2039634"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=2039634#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2039100" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
L'immensit√© has a moderate projection on my best male friend and a wear time of about 8 hours. It is slightly overpriced for what you're getting but it is still quite good. I received L‚ÄôImmensit√© as a gift and I have worn it alongside Tygar, BDC, Percival, Sedley, Afternoon Swim, and Imagination. In my opinion, it borrows and shares a bit with them all. The magnificent grapefruit openings of Tygar &amp; Afternoon Swim. The intoxicating &amp; ethereal quality of Imagination without the tealeaf (which I prefer). The versatility and depth of BDC EDP (with Cascalone replacing Incense). The aromatic &amp; fresh spiciness of the PDM ‚Äúblues‚Äù but even smoother.<br />
<br />
In terms of pure AROMA, it‚Äôs hard to dismiss L‚ÄôImmensit√© as an ALL-TIME GREAT. I browsed two LV stores last month where the sales staff noted their preference for it as their best men‚Äôs fragrance.<br />
<br />
What may be even more impressive, you could call this a linear scent, because (for myself) it just does NOT dry down for 6-9 hours and this includes the very high-quality citrus opening and aquatic heart notes. (What I find with Tygar and its clones (e.g. Turathi Blue) is that they gradually drydown to a heavy spice/amber that I do not like.<br />
<br />
In terms of VALUE. since I own a bottle of L‚ÄôImmensit√© now, the cost to refill 100ml will be comparable to buying another bottle of BDC EDP noting that L'Immensite is higher quality (niche level), has more longevity, and takes fewer sprays.<br />
<br />
I am very glad I received it as a gift because I would have put the money instead towards 2-3 other designer alternatives and not experienced what I have in hand now and IT IS SPECIAL.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; -5ml sample<br />
-Citrus opening is nice, I don't get much grapefruit, expensive smelling calone +a light non-headache inducing ambroxan + bergamot and ginger combo<br />
-Calone note is really good, not too cologne-ny, reminds me B&amp;BW ocean hand sanitizer.<br />
-Very quickly gets to the mid. Rosemary and geranium come first, gives a nice green sweet, slightly sharp effect. Geranium is in the background making it vaguely floral/masculine. <br />
-Nice in the air, especially the calone + rosemary + ambroxan combo<br />
-Close to skin, something is mildly bordering on the savory/challenging. Doesn't cross over, but almost gets there on some up close sniffs<br />
-About an hour in, still have the sharp green from rosemary, ambroxan, but the sage is coming in with a smokey edge I don't like. <br />
-Dry down is quite smokey on my skin, sharp from rosemary, ambroxan is there, never headache-y like afternoon swim ambroxan. Not super pleasant or very sweet.<br />
-Opening and early mid is 7.5/10, relatively unique<br />
-Late mid I would never wear, 2.5/10<br />
-Deep dry down, the smokiness is gone, as with most of the rosemary. Has the profondo/polo deep blue parfum dry down exactly, with a touch of rosemary<br />
-Performance is strong, still coming off my skin 4-5 hours in, lasts around 8-10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1881416"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1881416#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1880059" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1758842" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Lukasssss"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1657553"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Lukasssss" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1758842ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1758842" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1657553">Lukasssss</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-13">02/13/23 04:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Heavenly fresh aromatic opening that is characterized by ginger, bitter grapefruit, and herbs. It feels aquatic and green.<br />
Ambery notes start to come alive in the dry down - this is where the magic happens.<br />
The ambery base notes add a slight warmth to the otherwise cold, fresh, aquatic, and herbal notes. The result is something that reminds me of a late summer sunset over the ocean. The last rays of sun color the sky in orange as a reminder of the warmth and brightness it brings while the cold waves hit the cliffs and the sporadic gusts of wind escort the smell of close-by vegetation. <br />
Very versatile fragrance but best fit for the warmer part of the year.<br />
The scent is nice and I love it, but I would not pay full price for a bottle. In my opinion, many cheaper similar fragrances do the job almost as good, and it is not worth an extra $100-$150 for somebody with a limited budget. 7,5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; On the bright side though, it would appeal to a much larger audience, and outlasts most colognes with a similar vibe in terms of performance. Like seriously, I can smell this on my clothes up to three days after I‚Äôm done wearing them. <br />
<br />
This is almost a much more niche-feeling version of Bleu de Chanel, heavy on citrus and amber from opening to drydown. The heart starts to project a salty marine quality, while the drydown emphasizes the ambery vibe. Although it is fresh-leaning and qualifies as a ‚Äúblue‚Äù shower-gel-like cologne, L‚ÄôImmensit√© smells high-quality, elegant, and bougie. It is a bit mature (just a bit), but by all accounts it‚Äôs got heavy seduction power. I‚Äôd personally recommend using this for more formal occasions in the summer, or for a fancy sunset date in warmer weather. There may be similar options for much lower prices, but I like putting my money into quality options, and you‚Äôd definitely get quality with L‚ÄôImmensit√©.<br />
<br />
SCORE: 90%<br />
<br />
--<br />
<br />
UPDATE 5/20/2023: I've got a bit of a pro-tip for you-- if you layer L'Immensit√© with Acqua di Gio Profumo (two colognes which bear a deep similarity to each other), the resulting scent off your skin is sublime. I don't know which part of my ass I pulled this idea from, but I tried it, and surprisingly, it smelled so good.<br />
<br />
UPDATE 9/3/2023: my love for this fragrance might have decreased just a bit. Maybe it's because my tastes are changing, maybe because my bank account is emptier than my soul right now--whatever it is, I no longer believe that this fragrance is worth the almost $300 price tag it sells for. If you can find this for under $200, then great--honestly, go for it because it is still a superb and versatile fragrance to own on any occasion. However, for the retail price, I would encourage you to seek more artistic and creative fragrances with unique vibes and a nicer olfactive journey. However, nothing against L'Immensite at all--honestly, I probably just opened my mouth because I'm now a broke b*tch.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1732211"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1732211#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1718638" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; They smell identical.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1708786"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1708786#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1706818" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/504727">Ricks44</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-11">12/11/22 03:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If Boss Bottled and Ambre Nuit had a baby.<br />
<br />
This is basically a high end Boss Bottled. Sharp, fruity, masculine. Smells amazing. The opening is quite possibly one of the best Ive smelt. It does linger throughout the lifespan but not as prominent. It dries down to a slightly old school  musk/patchouli combo. This part I'm not totally keen on. Still nice but does slip into generic/cologne vibes.<br />
<br />
I dont really see it as a blue scent at all. It smells festive. Apple, spices, cinnamon, rose, amber. It does have a watery feel in the air so maybe that's why people are saying its a blue scent. To me it reminds me of the first time I smelt Boss Bottled on a friend when I was a kid at school. I literally hounded him until he revealed his fragrance. <br />
<br />
In a similar way to Boss Bottled, it gets quite boring quickly. Though it does a job &amp; does it well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1706818"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1706818#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1696832" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And it isn't really any surprised given they share the same perfumer. Take that grapefruit + ginger + ambery woods from Tygar and add marine salt and some herbals and you have L'Immensite. There's a bit of added depth but also draws it close to the generic bleu/blue genre of fragrances. Performance is also subdued unless you go a bit heavy on the trigger. However this comes at the expense of being synthetic and screechy so I wouldn't recommend doing so. <br />
<br />
I prefer Tygar as there's beauty it its simplicity. L'Immensite tries a bit too hard but honestly I'd probably pick up whichever can be bought for a better deal at the time as they are quite similar.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Of the 250+ bottles I've purchased over the past decade, this is the first time I paid full retail for a bottle. It's that good. This has some similarities to Bvlgari Tygar including the perfumer and that specific grapefruit note with ambroxan, but I much prefer L'Immensit√© over Tygar. This is more of a complete fragrance and an absolute masterpiece. L'Immensit√© differentiates itself with a more subdued grapefruit note and a lot more going on overall, including a prominent, effervescent ginger note and an overall airiness from the combination of all the middle notes. All of the ingredients blend together beautifully for a final product that just smells like pure luxury without the arrogance. It's very long lasting and projects well without ever feeling loud or in your face. I only wish I had discovered this sooner, but I'm not the type to ever go into a Louis Vuitton store, although now I'm sure I will go in eventually to refill my bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Also, there is no lemon rind ‚Äî it's Bergamot. The Grapefruit and Ambroxan are distinctively noticeable and prevalent in this fragrance. While the Grapefruit note dissipates rather quickly, the Ambroxan note remains linear, as it should for a base note.<br />
<br />
Personally, I think today's innovation standards in perfumery are a joke, best left for snowflakes and people who can't tell the difference between a fart and a leaking gas line. Having said that, this fragrance does not lie within the boundaries of standing the test of time. It is meant to be worn as a signature scent ‚Äî not to be sitting on the shelf for an extended period of time, or decanted (you never know what you're getting with those, anyway). Not to be worn in excess, as the Ambroxan can otherwise be overpowering. Therefore, my recommendation is to spray lightly, and not to be used as a clubbing fragrance. L‚ÄôImmensit√© is sophistication, and money in a bottle. Hence, the price point. However, Louis Vuitton does provide a nice discount for refills. Overall, an outstanding fragrance for people who don't mind the price point, and you won't smell like everyone else. 10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1666526"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1666526#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1664961" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1283557">malcolmtanyt</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-06-06">06/06/21 11:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Louis Vuitton L'immensite.. probably the only fragrance i have paid retail for ever since i got into fragrances.<br />
<br />
It was a difficult choice because i was deciding between this and Ombre Nomade, but luckily i have a good SA at Louis Vuitton that pushes me vials of Ombre Nomade samples every time i pop by the boutique (perks of spending too much money on unneccessary stuff there lol), and i discovered that if i ever purchase a full bottle of ON, it would take me 3 generations to finish the entire 100ml bottle. A 2ml sample vial lasts me 6 months lol.<br />
<br />
L'immensite, while it might smell pretty generic and mainstream, is really well blended - you can detect it's price tag just by its smell, even if you are not into fragrances. Louis Vuitton really went full on with their creations and didn't cut corners when it came to quality ingredients.<br />
<br />
I hate ginger in general but the ginger in this blends and complements the sparkling bergamot and slightly bitter grapefruit extremely well.<br />
<br />
This fragrance also project pretty well and lasts the entire day, albeit you might need to reapply at mid-day if you want it to continue projecting till you get home.<br />
<br />
I work in a climate-controlled environment most of the days, at the ratio of ladies to men is almost 5:1 so believe me when i tell you the ladies love it.<br />
<br />
Those who ridicule this are probably people who cannot afford it - trust me, i balked at coughing out the retail price ofr this bottle since i'm someone who is always searching for good deals on discounters but i have not regretted it ever since i swiped my card at the boutique because this fragrance just smells that good and it makes me happy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1314540" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="angelocsmanna"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1286593"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="angelocsmanna" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1314540ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1314540" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1286593">angelocsmanna</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-03-26">03/26/21 14:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Extremely underrated cologne solely due to its resemblance to basic blue scents yet this could not be further from the truth.<br />
While it is not the most complex / challenging scent nor is it  fully packed with natural compounds (which scent is nowadays), it is an attention grabbing crowd pleaser. It smells well blended and of high quality synthetic compounds, a bit harsh at the first spray but the edges round off a little in a few minutes. <br />
<br />
My best description of it (which I am surprised not more have picked up on): think YSL Kouros‚Äô musky amber, slightly cleaner and with a much much better blend of citrus and aromatic components.<br />
 A fruity sour grapefruit opening mixed with a spicy aromatic aquatic feeling, all resting on a very prominent salty musk-ambergris (ambroxan). The ambergris sort of resembles the one found in Profumi del Forte‚Äôs Ambra Mediterranea: salty wet and warm. This  scent evokes the feelings of relaxing on a boat on a humid summer day in the Mediterranean, you‚Äôre in the middle of the sea at sundown with a warm wind blowing off the surface of the water, filling your lungs with the sea‚Äôs essence.<br />
<br />
People, especially women, will notice you in the air and they love it from my experience, it‚Äôs clean sharp smelling but with a musky dirty touch that gives it an edge over a basic woody aromatic/ chypre  like BdC or Aventus. On skin it lasts the whole day, projects for a couple of hours quite strongly (probably even longer since we all underestimate ambroxan‚Äôs sillage power). On clothes it lasts days.<br />
It is an expensive purchase but this is one of the few fragrances I have actually repurchased (refilled at half price) coming from a maniac who has bought everything from basic blue scents to Rojas and Clive Christians. <br />
<br />
I think it is an excellent fragrance for daily use, especially at night time in summer/autumn. I discovered it on my friend 2.5 years ago on a high heat evening in summer while I stepped in his car; one of the few fragrances that I asked someone ‚Äúwhat is that? it smells f****ng amazing‚Äù and bought the bottle a few days later. For me to give a compliment, the scent must be something I hadn‚Äôt sampled in over 300 perfumes I have tried and it must be at the level of some heavyweight champions.<br />
Highly recommend it. At least sample it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="1314540"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=1314540#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent956369" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/244676">scott.lauze</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-06-27">06/27/18 11:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't really understand the reviews posted so far.  I find this to be quite beautiful, masculine in a slightly retro way, a classic out-of-the-shower aromatic fougere in the same vein as Azzaro pour homme or Ormonde Jayne Zizan.<br />
<br />
I never get random compliments on scents, and I got two the first day I wore this.  Is it ground-breaking? no.  Does it smell niche? no.  But it is comfortable and easy-wearing, long lasting (8 hours) with the most projection of any of the new masculine Vuitton releases.<br />
<br />
I do not get any dirtiness or civet.  The ginger and amber add a warmth that carries it into oriental territory, especially in the drydown.  It is not an ambroxan freshie.  It has a liquid, clear texture; not dense, scratchy or fizzy.  I see no similarity to Aventus, and it doesn't have the complexity of a Roja.  The grapefruit reminds me a little of TdH, but l'Immensit√© is not quite as austere.<br />
<br />
This is a winner for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="49751"comment_id="956369"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/L-Immensite-49751.html?ccid=956369#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="49751" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
